source /mnt/c/Users/Research/Documents/GitHub/MAXI-J1535/code/xspec_related/common.tcl
statistic pgstat
setp back on
energies 0.01 200. 1000 log
model tbabs(simpl(diskbb))
3.2107 , 2 2 5 5
2.0 0.05 1.1 1.4 3.5 4.0
0.1 0.1 0.001 0.01 0.9 1.0
1
, , 0.2 0.2 2 3
, , 0.1 0.1 1000000000 1000000000
freeze 1
chatter 5 10
parallel leven 2
fit 250
n

tclout stat
scan $xspec_tclout "%f" pgstat
tclout dof
scan $xspec_tclout "%f" dof
set redpgstat [expr $pgstat / $dof]
log /mnt/c/Users/Research/Documents/GitHub/MAXI-J1535/code/spectral_routines/jan-29-simpl/logs/1050360103_0_before_error.txt
show data
show param
show fit
log none
if {$redpgstat < 3} {
set error_array [_pct_get_error_list {2 3 4 5} 2.706]
set error_log_file [open /mnt/c/Users/Research/Documents/GitHub/MAXI-J1535/code/spectral_routines/jan-29-simpl/logs/1050360103_0_errorlog.txt w]
set header_string "value,lower_err,upper_err,err_str" 
puts $error_log_file $header_string
foreach item $error_array {
set item [join $item ,]
puts $error_log_file $item
}
close $error_log_file
}
quit
y
sleep 0.5

}
